Local State üì≤
You can now create variables that can save the state of your app without needing to store data in Firebase or elsewhere. üëå

These values can be updated with an action to build interactive experiences. You can even choose which values to be saved on the device so that the state is not reset if the app is restarted in the future.

Custom Actions üßô
For those of you who want to be able to add functionality using custom code, this new feature unlocks a lot of possibilities. Custom Actions allow you to import any pub.dev (Dart and Flutter) package and write custom code you can run as an action.

Once you've added a custom action, it's seamless to call it when the user interacts with your app from the FlutterFlow UI, it shows up along with actions that are built-in to FlutterFlow! ü™Ñ
17:39
Empty List Component üíé
You can now show a custom component when your query returns no results. While this is a small refinement, it can have a big impact on user experience!

Using a custom component you can give users more information on what is happening and guide them on what steps to take. For example, you could tell users that their cart is empty and give them the option to browse the menu.
